Subject: The Promise of FIRST

Dear Colleagues,

Please find attached the 1st announcement of the FIRST symposium, "the
promise of FIRST", to be held from 12-15 December in Spain. I hope you
will be able to attend.
At the next HIFI consortium meeting, March 23 and 24, we will discuss
the HIFI preparation for this meeting.

With best wishes for the New Year,

Thijs
